"a39523e4d4e7dd11739b4e0d65abe0d1a811efb6", "filename": "MapleCouponInstaller/src/maplecouponinstaller/MapleCouponInstaller.java", "status": "added", "additions": 300, "deletions": 0, "changes": 300, "blob_url": "https://github.com/ronancpl/HeavenMS/blob/e1c95352c808e47c852107a51a1f2cf3064fa5c7/MapleCouponInstaller/src/maplecouponinstaller/MapleCouponInstaller.java", "raw_url": "https://github.com/ronancpl/HeavenMS/raw/e1c95352c808e47c852107a51a1f2cf3064fa5c7/MapleCouponInstaller/src/maplecouponinstaller/MapleCouponInstaller.java", "contents_url": "https://api.github.com/repos/ronancpl/HeavenMS/contents/MapleCouponInstaller/src/maplecouponinstaller/MapleCouponInstaller.java?ref=e1c95352c808e47c852107a51a1f2cf3064fa5c7", "patch": "@@ -0,0 +1,300 @@\n+/*\n+ * To change this license header, choose License Headers in Project Properties.\n+ * To change this template file, choose Tools | Templates\n+ * and open the template in the editor.\n+ */\n+package maplecouponinstaller;\n+\n+import java.io.*;\n+import java.sql.Connection;\n+import java.sql.DriverManager;\n+import java.sql.PreparedStatement;\n+import java.sql.SQLException;\n+\n+/**\n+ *\n+ * @author RonanLana\n+ * \n+ * This application gathers information about the Cash Shop EXP & DROP coupons, such\n+ * as applied rates, active times of day and days of week and dumps them in a SQL\n+ * table, in which will be used by the server.\n+ * \n+ */\n+public class MapleCouponInstaller {\n+    static String host = \"jdbc:mysql://localhost:3306/maplesolaxia\";\n+    static String driver = \"com.mysql.jdbc.Driver\";\n+    static String username = \"root\";\n+    static String password = \"\";\n+    \n+    static Connection con = null;\n+    static InputStreamReader fileReader = null;\n+    static BufferedReader bufferedReader = null;\n+    static byte status = 0;\n+    static int itemId = -1, itemMultiplier = 1, startHour = -1, endHour = -1, activeDay = 0;\n+\n+    private static String getName(String token) {\n+        int i, j;\n+        char[] dest;\n+        String d;\n+\n+        i = token.lastIndexOf(\"name\");\n+        if(i < 0) return \"\";\n+        \n+        i = token.indexOf(\"\\\"\", i) + 1; //lower bound of the string\n+        j = token.indexOf(\"\\\"\", i);     //upper bound\n+\n+        dest = new char[8];\n+        token.getChars(i, j, dest, 0);\n+\n+        d = new String(dest);\n+        return(d);\n+    }\n+    \n+    private static String getNodeValue(String token) {\n+        int i, j;\n+        char[] dest;\n+        String d;\n+\n+        i = token.lastIndexOf(\"value=\");\n+        i = token.indexOf(\"\\\"\", i) + 1; //lower bound of the string\n+        j = token.indexOf(\"\\\"\", i);     //upper bound\n+        \n+        if(j - i < 1) return \"\";\n+        \n+        dest = new char[j - i];\n+        token.getChars(i, j, dest, 0);\n+\n+        d = new String(dest);\n+        return(d);\n+    }\n+\n+    private static void forwardCursor(int st) {\n+        String line = null;\n+\n+        try {\n+            while(status >= st && (line = bufferedReader.readLine()) != null) {\n+                simpleToken(line);\n+            }\n+        }\n+        catch(Exception e) {\n+            e.printStackTrace();\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    private static void simpleToken(String token) {\n+        if(token.contains(\"/imgdir\")) {\n+            status -= 1;\n+        }\n+        else if(token.contains(\"imgdir\")) {\n+            status += 1;\n+        }\n+    }\n+    \n+    private static int getDayOfWeek(String day) {\n+        switch(day) {\n+            case \"SUN\":\n+                return 1;\n+                \n+            case \"MON\":\n+                return 2;\n+                    \n+            case \"TUE\":\n+                return 3;\n+                        \n+            case \"WED\":\n+                return 4;\n+                            \n+            case \"THU\":\n+                return 5;\n+                                \n+            case \"FRI\":\n+                return 6;\n+                                    \n+            case \"SAT\":\n+                return 7;\n+                \n+            default:\n+                return 0;\n+        }\n+    }\n+    \n+    private static void processHourTimeString(String time) {\n+        startHour = Integer.parseInt(time.substring(4, 6));\n+        endHour = Integer.parseInt(time.substring(7, 9));\n+    }\n+    \n+    private static void processDayTimeString(String time) {\n+        String day = time.substring(0, 2);\n+        int d = getDayOfWeek(day);\n+        \n+        activeDay |= (1 << d);\n+    }\n+\n+    private static void loadTimeFromCoupon(int st) {\n+        System.out.println(\"Loading coupon id \" + itemId + \". Rate: \" + itemMultiplier + \"x.\");\n+        \n+        String line = null;\n+        try {\n+            startHour = -1;\n+            endHour = -1;\n+            activeDay = 0;\n+            \n+            String time = null;\n+            while((line = bufferedReader.readLine()) != null) {\n+                simpleToken(line);\n+                if(status < st) break;\n+                \n+                time = getNodeValue(line);\n+                processDayTimeString(time);\n+                \n+                simpleToken(line);\n+            }\n+            \n+            if(time != null) {\n+                processHourTimeString(time);\n+                \n+                PreparedStatement ps = con.prepareStatement(\"INSERT INTO nxcoupons (couponid, rate, activeday, starthour, endhour) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?)\");\n+                ps.setInt(1, itemId);\n+                ps.setInt(2, itemMultiplier);\n+                ps.setInt(3, activeDay);\n+                ps.setInt(4, startHour);\n+                ps.setInt(5, endHour);\n+                ps.execute();\n+\n+                ps.close();\n+            }\n+        }\n+        catch(SQLException | IOException e) {\n+            e.printStackTrace();\n+        }\n+    }\n+\n+    private static void translateToken(String token) {\n+        String d;\n+\n+        if(token.contains(\"/imgdir\")) {\n+            status -= 1;\n+        }\n+        else if(token.contains(\"imgdir\")) {\n+            if(status == 1) {           //getting ItemId\n+                d = getName(token);\n+                itemId = Integer.parseInt(d);\n+            }\n+            else if(status == 2) {\n+                d = getName(token);\n+\n+                if(!d.contains(\"info\")) {\n+                    forwardCursor(status);\n+                }\n+            }\n+            else if(status == 3) {\n+                d = getName(token);\n+\n+                if(!d.contains(\"time\")) {\n+
